569   *  Delay: '<S1>/Delay'



570   *  Gain: '<S1>/\delta t'



571   *  Gain: '<S1>/beta'



572   *  Sum: '<S1>/Sum'



573   */



574  Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[0] = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0 -



575    0.075574973509759 * rtb_Normalization1[0];



576  Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[1] = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1 -



577    0.075574973509759 * rtb_Normalization1[1];



578  Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[2] = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2 -



579    0.075574973509759 * rtb_Normalization1[2];



580  Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[3] = (0.01 * rtb_Sum_j +



581    Madgwick_embedded_DW.Delay_DSTATE[3]) - 0.075574973509759 *



582    rtb_Normalization1[3];



583



584  /* MATLABSystem: '<S1>/Coordinate Transformation Conversion' */



585  rtb_Sum_g = 1.0 / sqrt(((Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[0] *



586    Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[0] + Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[1] *



587    Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[1]) + Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[2] *



588    Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[2]) + Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[3] *



589    Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[3]);



590  frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0 = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[0] * rtb_Sum_g;



591  frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1 = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[1] * rtb_Sum_g;



592  frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2 = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[2] * rtb_Sum_g;



593  frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_3 = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[3] * rtb_Sum_g;



594  rtb_Sum_g = (frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_3 +



595               frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0) * 2.0;



596  if (rtb_Sum_g > 1.0) {



597    rtb_Sum_g = 1.0;



598  }



599



600  c = rtb_Sum_g;



601  if (rtb_Sum_g < -1.0) {



602    c = -1.0;



603  }



604



605  rtb_Sum_g = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0;



606  CoordinateTransformationConvers = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1 *



607    frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1;



608  CoordinateTransformationConve_0 = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2 *



609    frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2;



610  CoordinateTransformationConve_1 = frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_3 *



611    frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_3;



612  Madgwick_embedded_B.CoordinateTransformationConvers[0] = rt_atan2d_snf



613    ((frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_3 -



614      frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0) * -2.0, ((rtb_Sum_g



615       - CoordinateTransformationConvers) - CoordinateTransformationConve_0) +



616     CoordinateTransformationConve_1);



617  Madgwick_embedded_B.CoordinateTransformationConvers[1] = asin(c);



618  Madgwick_embedded_B.CoordinateTransformationConvers[2] = rt_atan2d_snf



619    ((frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_1 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_2 -



620      frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_3 * frac12S_Ehatq_estt1_idx_0) * -2.0, ((rtb_Sum_g



621       + CoordinateTransformationConvers) - CoordinateTransformationConve_0) -



622     CoordinateTransformationConve_1);



623



624  /* End of MATLABSystem: '<S1>/Coordinate Transformation Conversion' */



625



626  /* SignalConversion generated from: '<Root>/MATLAB Animation' */



627  Madgwick_embedded_B.TmpSignalConversionAtMATLABAnim[0] = 0.0;



628  Madgwick_embedded_B.TmpSignalConversionAtMATLABAnim[1] = 0.0;



629  Madgwick_embedded_B.TmpSignalConversionAtMATLABAnim[2] = 0.0;



630



631  /* Update for Delay: '<S1>/Delay' */



632  Madgwick_embedded_DW.Delay_DSTATE[0] = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[0];



633  Madgwick_embedded_DW.Delay_DSTATE[1] = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[1];



634  Madgwick_embedded_DW.Delay_DSTATE[2] = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[2];



635  Madgwick_embedded_DW.Delay_DSTATE[3] = Madgwick_embedded_B.S_Eq_estt[3];



636



637  /* Update absolute time for base rate */



638  /* The "clockTick0" counts the number of times the code of this task has



639   * been executed. The absolute time is the multiplication of "clockTick0"



640   * and "Timing.stepSize0". Size of "clockTick0" ensures timer will not



641   * overflow during the application lifespan selected.



642   */



643  Madgwick_embedded_M->Timing.t[0] =



644    ((time_T)(++Madgwick_embedded_M->Timing.clockTick0)) *



645    Madgwick_embedded_M->Timing.stepSize0;



646



647  {



648    /* Update absolute timer for sample time: [0.01s, 0.0s] */



649    /* The "clockTick1" counts the number of times the code of this task has



650     * been executed. The resolution of this integer timer is 0.01, which is the step size



651     * of the task. Size of "clockTick1" ensures timer will not overflow during the



652     * application lifespan selected.



653     */



654    Madgwick_embedded_M->Timing.clockTick1++;



655  }



656}
